name:T‚Äçu‚Äçp‚Äçp‚Äçi‚Äçl
info:Superior Garden-view  Room
info:Stayed in August 2021
info:Family
info:1 Review
rating:5
posted:Posted August 19, 2021
msg:I really enjoyed my stay. The hotel is very spacious, clean and modern. It's quite pretty here, as the place is surrounded by beautifully landscaped grounds. My room overlooked the views of the beach and the  lush green grounds.  Woke up to the tweeting of the birds and calming sounds of the beach waves. Very very nice! The room was super clean and well-maintained. Overall, the staff was helpul from the start. However, I don't speak Chinese very well, so I had hoped that the entire staff would speak some English as this is an IHG property, but this was not the case. Thank goodness for Carson, the only one who could speak English. He was absolutely professional and welcoming and played a roll in making sure I enjoyed my time there. He was very quick to reply to my questions and promptly provided assistance when I had a specific request regarding the room. The breakfast buffet was lovely, as they offer a variety of food to suit most tastes. The only thing I would say I didn'tlove is the pricy buffet dinner. But the good thing is there is also a non-buffet Chinese restaurant so it was nice to have this choice. There is also a third restauarant but it was temporarily closed.  Another amenity I liked are the huge pools. They were also very clean and well-maintained. The private access to the  beach was perfect, situated just outside of the hotel, about a couple of minutes walk. The beach is clean and although the waves were rough and not suitable for swimming there were other activities: take a ride on the boat, go on a jet ski or go water gliding. You can also rent an umbrella and chairs, but unfortunately, the chair is a simple, small plastic one and not the most comfortable and definitely not as relaxing. Overall, I had a great experience and definitely plan to return and stay  here again.

The ride-hailing service here is very fast, but after you grab it, they will call you and tell you that they may not be able to pick you up at that time, but you can find other friends to pick you up. The attitude is very good. Uninformed tourists will think that they are very sincere. In fact, they are just occupying your order. Before departure, they will tell you that they can't pick you up. In addition, if a friend can charter a car to pick you up for 100 yuan, the original order is 50 yuan. It will be doubled directly. Don‚Äôt be fooled. When encountering this situation, when you first say that you may not be able to accept the order, directly ask the other party to cancel the order immediately, otherwise you will complain to Didi customer service. After they cancel, there will be other offers immediately. The car owner takes the order and calls to confirm whether he can pick you up on time. After all, there are still good drivers. You can't let a group of such people ruin the entire hitchhiking drivers in Yangjiang City. This happened to me when I arrived and left. It can be seen that it is not the case. For example, if Yangjiang Cultural Tourism cannot rectify this situation, more and more guests will complain during the peak tourist period. The scenery of Hailing Island is really good, and service determines success or failure.

The front desk service was very friendly and we upgraded to a sea view room for free. The hotel's architectural layout is grand and dignified, as if it is embracing the South China Sea with outstretched arms. Looking around, you can see the whirling green coconut trees, the blue sea and sky, and the silver sand beach stretching to the end of the sky like a jade belt. Under the starry sky at night, white waves crash on the shore, singing softly, and falling asleep on the waves.
Room: spacious, clean and comfortable. Southeast Asian decorative style, natural and simple. Push open the oversized sliding door of the bathroom, lie in the bathtub, feel the sea breeze and listen to the sound of the waves.
Catering: The breakfast buffet is rich in variety and hygienic. The Western restaurant has a hot pot buffet for dinner. There is a food street 700 meters away from the hotel. The level of excitement is not as good as that of Zhapo. It's a pity that the deluxe sea view room is actually facing the sea as shown in the picture, but the eyesight is not wide enough. The superior sea view room may be more open horizontally. Moreover, due to the festival, the house price has increased a lot and it is a bit expensive.
It is more convenient to live in the east wing. There is a children's playground, indoor swimming pool, sauna room, and free parking.
Meals: The buffet is so-so. The number of dishes is not very rich. Personally, I would like to eat more salmon, lamb chops, and lychees. The dishes that were originally given away according to the person‚Äôs hair ticket were also not available because of the festival manager. It‚Äôs okay to eat when there are discounts, but The festival price has doubled and there is no cost performance. The taste of the Chinese restaurant is okay. As for the seafood stalls, because there is no shortage of seafood in the place where I live, I don't order too much seafood and I don't get caught in the water.
Generally speaking, you can't go wrong with choosing a good hotel for traveling with children, and the children also had a great time, and will come again if there is a more suitable opportunity in the future.

name:J‚Äçi‚Äça‚Äço‚Äçs‚Äçh‚Äçe‚Äçn‚Äçg‚ÄçS‚Äça‚Äçm‚ÄçG‚Äço‚Äçr‚Äçd‚Äçe‚Äçl‚Äça
info:Deluxe Family Friendly Room - Near Pool
info:Stayed in June 2021
info:Family
info:1 Review
rating:5
posted:Posted July 1, 2021
msg:Before leaving, I looked at several Internet celebrity hotels in Hailing Island, and finally chose the old brand. I have no regrets at all! That's great!

For the seaside hotel, the surrounding facilities are complete. There are convenience stores, restaurants, hospitals, and so on. There are also shared electric cars next to the hotel. If you don't want to drive, it is very pleasant to ride a small electric donkey to eat seafood or something.

The lobby of the hotel is very big. Although the hardware looks a little bit historical, it is well maintained, the stay is very comfortable, and the hygiene is very meticulous.

I stayed in the open-style poolside parent-child room on the first floor. The room has a large sense of space. There is enough space for the two children to make noise. The corners of the tables and chairs in the room are all posted with child protection corners, which is very intimate! There are also children's toothbrushes, slippers and small bathrobes. The huge round bathtub in the bathroom is amazing! The outdoor swimming pool space is quite large, and children and adults have fun in it. You will occasionally see one or two ants next to the swimming pool, but it is understandable that the surrounding environment is well maintained. Close the windows at night, otherwise there will be mosquitoes, although there are electric mosquito lamps and liquid mosquito coils in the room.
It‚Äôs worth suggesting that there is a small tent in the room, which should be decorated for the parent-child theme, but that tent is unstable. The child can easily fall down when touched. I put the tent away for safety. Actually, the parent-child room Some toys and dolls can be properly placed in the room, which makes children happier and safer than this kind of tent.

The hotel has two swimming pools, indoor and outdoor, and the water is very clean. The beach is just outside, and it takes about 5 minutes to walk out. Walking out of the hotel, the beach passes through the hotel‚Äôs garden. The greening is very good, but you must spray mosquito repellent water in advance. The mosquitoes are very poisonous. Seeing that there are hot springs, it should be because the epidemic situation has not been open. The sand on the beach is very fine, and the entire beach is also very clean. We go there on weekdays, or maybe because of the epidemic, there are no people and it is very comfortable. The beach in front of the hotel cannot go to the sea. If you want to go to the sea, you have to pay to the beach next to it. The waves in this sea are very big, and it is not suitable for children to go into the sea. I think it is very good to dig small shells and small sand crabs to pile sand on the shore.

I have to mention this trip, the hotel's service is really good! Absolutely worthy of the brand, the best service I have ever stayed in this year. Every employee is very friendly, polite and smiling. As soon as we got off the car, Bellboy helped us with the luggage. He mentioned the room from the check in and kept mentioning the car for us when we left.
Especially Miss Hai Ling at the front desk, arranged for me super, and the service was very caring and in place. Hailing helped me upgrade my room, also helped me apply for a late check-out, and provided me with a free ticket to the vip beach. I always come to play without making a strategy, Hailing will tell me the fun places around. The day of check-in is my birthday. The birthday decorations are made in the room early. Hailing will confirm with me the time when the cake will be delivered to the room, which is very comfortable.
During the stay, whenever there is a need, call the guest service center, which can provide what you need in less than 5 minutes, which is quite efficient. During the epidemic prevention period, Anxin Packs are also intimately provided, including disposable hand sanitizers, masks, and disinfectant wipes. In the evening, sweet water was also given, which is great!
The aunt who is in charge of room hygiene is also quite responsible. She will also consult and see where improvements can be made and write greeting cards. There will be a little leaf floating down in the outdoor swimming pool, and there will be a cleaning uncle to help clean the pool.
This kind of service really deserves a five-star rating!
It's a pity that the buffet is only open on weekends, and we didn't enjoy it when we came. The breakfast buffet is open in the executive corridor. There are not many varieties, but the things are quite fresh.

Overall this is a great experience! I want to come again next time.
